match(a:prescription where a.name = 'Prescription_477')-[e:contain]->(b:medicine),(c:prescription where c.name = 'Prescription_341')-[e2:contain]->(d:medicine) return a, b, c, d
with p as (select * from (VALUES(78,16,'famale'),(48,14,'male')) as t(age,id,gender))MATCH (a:teacher WHERE a.gender = p.gender) <-[e:department_has_teacher ]-(b:department WHERE b.name = '法学院') RETURN a, b 
match(a:orders)<-[e:cancel]-(b:buyer where b.name='孙思琪') return a, b
match(a:goods | seller where name = '杜若涵')-[e]-(b:buyer) return a.name, b.name
match(a:company) return a
with p as (select * from (VALUES(237),(545),(330),(225)) as t(id)) MATCH (a:seller WHERE a.id = p.id) -[e:seller_has_goods ]->(b:goods) RETURN e 
match(a:publisher where a.name = '李若涵')-[e]-(b:reader), (a:publisher)-[e2:publish]->(c:book) return a, b, c
match(a:comment where a.id <= 91)-[e:belong]->(b:film)-[e2:has]->(c:tag) return b.name as b_name, c.name as c_name
match(a:city)-[e:contain]->(b:company) let b.peopleNumber = MAX((b:company)<-[e2:contain]-(c:city) => c.name) match(b:company)-[e3:belong]->(d:city) return b.peopleNumber, d
match(a where (a.weight < 329 or a.name = 'Prescription_408') and a.name = 'Prescription_372')-[e:prescription_contain_medicine]->(b where (b.weight BETWEEN 282 AND 540) and b.name <> '散利痛' and (b.price is null)) return e

match(a:person where a.name='杜宏')-[e:parent]->(b)<-[e2:parent]-(c:person where c.name='周思琪') return b limit 50
match(a:company where a.name='蚂蚁集团')-[e]-(b:person | company | account) return b.id, b.gender, b.name
match(a:patient where name = '孙科')-[e:accept]->(b:prescription)-[e2:contain]->(c:medicine) return c.price
match(a:book where a.name='悲惨世界')-[e]-(b:author) return b.salary
match(a:university where MAX(a.level) < 2)-[e:has]->(b:department)-[e2:has]->(c:teacher) return b.name as b_name, c.name as c_name
